$.fn.responsiveTabs = function () {
	return this.each(function () {
		var el = $(this),
			tabs = el.find("dt"),
			content = el.find("dd"),
			placeholder = $(
				'<div class="homenews-tabs-placeholder"></div>'
			).insertAfter(el);

		tabs.on("click", function () {
			var tab = $(this);
			if(tab.hasClass("active")) {
				tab.removeClass("active");
			}else{
				tab.addClass("active");
			}
			tabs.not(tab).removeClass("active");

			placeholder.html(tab.next().html());
		});

		if($(window).width() > 767) {
			tabs.filter(":first").trigger("click");
		}

	});
};

$(".homenews-tabs").responsiveTabs();

        // Get browser width
        function getBrowserWidth() {
            return Math.max(
                document.body.scrollWidth,
                document.documentElement.scrollWidth,
                document.body.offsetWidth,
                document.documentElement.offsetWidth,
                document.documentElement.clientWidth
            );
        }
        var browserWidth = getBrowserWidth();

        // Load Desktop/Mobile list depending on browser width
        if (browserWidth >= '768') {
            videoList = videoListDesktop;
        } else {
            videoList = videoListMobile;
        }

        // Play random Video

                    .catch(error => {
                        // Auto-play was prevented
                        // Show paused UI.
                    });

            /* Fade on scroll */

            var totalHeight = $(window).outerHeight();
            var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();

            setTimeout(function() {
                var scrollPercent = ((totalHeight - scrollTop) / totalHeight);
                //console.log(scrollPercent);

                    scrollPercent = .15; // Max Opacity

    function menuexpsearch() {

        jQuery.ajax({
            url: 'https://www.rimonlaw.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
            type: 'post',
            data: {
                action: 'data_fetch',
                keyword: jQuery('.menuexpsearch').val()
            },
            success: function(data) {
                jQuery('#menuexpsearchfetch').html(data);
                jQuery('.menuexpsearch-words').html(jQuery('.menuexpsearch').val());
                if (jQuery('.menuexpsearch').val() != '') {
                    jQuery('.menuexpsearchrelated').removeClass("hide");
                } else {
                    jQuery('.menuexpsearchrelated').addClass("hide");

                }
            }

        });

    }

    function menuteamsearch() {
        jQuery('.subnav-team .menuteamsearch').keyup(function() {
            //console.log('team');
            var i = jQuery(".subnav-team input").quicksearch(".team-member", {
                delay: 500,
                hide: function() {
                    jQuery(this).remove()
                },
                onAfter: function() {
                    var e;
                    jQuery(".subnav-team .results .team-member").length >= 1 ? jQuery(this).val().trim() && jQuery(".subnav-team .results-nav").show() : jQuery(this).val().trim() && jQuery(".subnav-team .results-nav").hide(), jQuery(".subnav-team #paging_container").pajinate({
                        item_container_id: ".results",
                        items_per_page: 6,
                        show_first_last: !1
                    })
                }
            });
            var minlength = 2;
            var value = jQuery(this).val();

            if (value.length >= minlength) {
                if (teamSearchRequest != null)
                    teamSearchRequest.abort();

                teamSearchRequest = jQuery.ajax({
                    url: ajaxurl,
                    type: 'post',
                    data: {
                        action: 'data_menuteam',
                        teammenuname: value
                    },
                    beforeSend: function() {
                        jQuery(".subnav-team .preloader").show();
                        jQuery(".subnav-team .results").empty();
                    },
                    success: function(data) {
                        jQuery(".subnav-team .preloader").hide(),
                            jQuery(".subnav-team .results").empty(),
                            jQuery(".subnav-team .results").append(data),
                            i.cache(),
                            jQuery(".subnav-team .results .team-member").length >= 1 ? jQuery(".subnav-team #noresults").hide() : jQuery(".subnav-team #noresults").show()
                    }

                });

            }

        });

    }
